import os
import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.distributed as dist
from torch.nn.parallel import DistributedDataParallel as DDP
from torch.utils.data.distributed import DistributedSampler
from torch.utils.data import Dataset, DataLoader
from torch.amp import autocast, GradScaler 
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from tqdm import tqdm
from timm.models.swin_transformer import SwinTransformerBlock, PatchMerging

# ==========================================
# 1. å·¥å…·å‡½æ•°: æ–­ç‚¹ç»­ä¼ 
# ==========================================
def save_checkpoint(epoch, model, optimizer, scaler, path="latest_checkpoint.pth"):
    checkpoint = {
        'epoch': epoch,
        'model_state_dict': model.module.state_dict(),
        'optimizer_state_dict': optimizer.state_dict(),
        'scaler_state_dict': scaler.state_dict(),
    }
    torch.save(checkpoint, path)

def load_checkpoint(model, optimizer, scaler, path="latest_checkpoint.pth"):
    if os.path.exists(path):
        map_location = {'cuda:%d' % 0: 'cuda:%d' % dist.get_rank()}
        checkpoint = torch.load(path, map_location=map_location)
        # å¦‚æœç»´åº¦ä¸åŒ¹é…ï¼ˆæ¯”å¦‚æ—§çš„8ç»´è½½å…¥æ–°çš„9ç»´ï¼‰ï¼Œä¼šåœ¨è¿™é‡ŒæŠ›é”™ã€‚
        # æ‰€ä»¥å¿…é¡»æ‰‹åŠ¨ rm latest_checkpoint.pth 
        model.module.load_state_dict(checkpoint['model_state_dict'])
        optimizer.load_state_dict(checkpoint['optimizer_state_dict'])
        scaler.load_state_dict(checkpoint['scaler_state_dict'])
        return checkpoint['epoch'] + 1
    return 0

# ==========================================
# 2. æ ¸å¿ƒæ¶æ„: Chopstick Swin-iTransformer
# ==========================================
class RevIN(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, num_features, eps=1e-5):
        super().__init__()
        # å¼ºåˆ¶åˆå§‹åŒ–ä¸ºè¾“å…¥ç»´åº¦ N
        self.affine_weight = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(1, 1, num_features))
        self.affine_bias = nn.Parameter(torch.zeros(1, 1, num_features))
        self.eps = eps

    def forward(self, x, mode='norm'):
        if mode == 'norm':
            self.mean = x.mean(1, keepdim=True).detach()
            self.stdev = torch.sqrt(x.var(1, keepdim=True, unbiased=False) + self.eps).detach()
            return (x - self.mean) / self.stdev * self.affine_weight + self.affine_bias
        else:
            return (x - self.affine_bias) / (self.affine_weight + self.eps) * self.stdev + self.mean

class Independent_Swin_iTransformer_V2(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, seq_len=96, num_vars=9, embed_dim=64, noise_std=0.02):
        super().__init__()
        self.num_vars = num_vars
        self.embed_dim = embed_dim
        self.noise_std = noise_std
        
        self.revin = RevIN(num_vars)
        
        # ğŸ¥¢ ç­·å­æŠ•å½±å±‚ (1x1 Pointwise Upscale)
        self.chopstick_proj = nn.Linear(3, embed_dim)

        # 9è·¯ç‹¬ç«‹ Swin ä¸“å®¶
        self.experts = nn.ModuleList([
            nn.ModuleDict({
                'stage1': nn.ModuleList([
                    SwinTransformerBlock(dim=embed_dim, input_resolution=(8, 12),
                                         num_heads=4, window_size=4,
                                         shift_size=0 if (i % 2 == 0) else 2) for i in range(2)
                ]),
                'merge': PatchMerging(dim=embed_dim),
                'stage2': nn.ModuleList([
                    SwinTransformerBlock(dim=embed_dim*2, input_resolution=(4, 6),
                                         num_heads=8, window_size=2,
                                         shift_size=0 if (i % 2 == 0) else 1) for i in range(2)
                ])
            }) for _ in range(num_vars)
        ])
        
        self.var_attn = nn.TransformerEncoderLayer(
            d_model=embed_dim * 2, nhead=8, dim_feedforward=512, 
            batch_first=True, norm_first=True
        )
        self.head = nn.Linear(embed_dim * 2, 1)
        self.final_gate = nn.Linear(num_vars, 1)

    def forward(self, x):
        B, L, N = x.shape
        x = self.revin(x, 'norm')
        
        # 1. ç­·å­ç”Ÿæˆé€»è¾‘
        c1 = x.unsqueeze(-1) # åŸå§‹
        idx2, idx3 = torch.randperm(L, device=x.device), torch.randperm(L, device=x.device)
        c2 = x[:, idx2, :].unsqueeze(-1) # æ‰“ä¹±
        
        # å·®åˆ†ç­·å­ (Local Momentum)
        c3 = torch.zeros_like(c1)
        c3[:, 1:, :, 0] = x[:, 1:, :] - x[:, :-1, :]
        
        feat_parallel = torch.cat([c1, c2, c3], dim=-1) # [B, L, N, 3]
        
        if self.training:
            feat_parallel = feat_parallel + torch.randn_like(feat_parallel) * self.noise_std
            
        # 2. ç‹¬ç«‹ Swin å¤„ç†
        expert_outputs = []
        for i in range(N):
            v = self.chopstick_proj(feat_parallel[:, :, i, :]).view(B, 8, 12, self.embed_dim)
            exp = self.experts[i]
            for blk in exp['stage1']: v = blk(v)
            v = exp['merge'](v)
            for blk in exp['stage2']: v = blk(v)
            expert_outputs.append(v.mean(dim=(1, 2)))
            
        # 3. iTransformer å˜é‡é—´æ³¨æ„åŠ›
        var_tokens = torch.stack(expert_outputs, dim=1) # [B, 9, 128]
        var_tokens = self.var_attn(var_tokens)
        
        # 4. å†³ç­–
        out_vars = self.head(var_tokens).squeeze(-1) # [B, 9]
        return self.final_gate(out_vars)

# ==========================================
# 3. æ•°æ®é›†: è‡ªåŠ¨å¯¹é½ N=9
# ==========================================
class BTCDatasetExpert(Dataset):
    def __init__(self, csv_path, flag='train'):
        df = pd.read_csv(csv_path)
        df.columns = [c.replace('"', '').strip() for c in df.columns]
        num_df = df.select_dtypes(include=[np.number])
        base_cols = [c for c in num_df.columns if 'time' not in c.lower()][:6]
        close = df[base_cols[3]]
        
        # 3ä¸ªä¸“å®¶æŒ‡æ ‡
        delta = close.diff()
        gain = delta.where(delta > 0, 0).rolling(14).mean()
        loss = delta.where(delta < 0, 0).abs().rolling(14).mean()
        df['f1'] = 100 - (100 / (1 + gain / (loss + 1e-5))) 
        df['f2'] = close.ewm(12).mean() - close.ewm(26).mean()
        df['f3'] = close.pct_change().rolling(20).std()
        
        feat_cols = (base_cols + ['f1', 'f2', 'f3'])[:9]
        if flag == 'train' and dist.get_rank() == 0:
            print(f"âœ… Features Loaded: {feat_cols}")

        data = df.iloc[30:][feat_cols].fillna(0).values.astype(np.float32)
        labels = (close.shift(-1) > close).astype(float).values[30:-1]
        
        data = data[:-1]
        data = (data - data.mean(0)) / (data.std(0) + 1e-5)
        
        split = int(len(data) * 0.8)
        self.data = data[:split] if flag == 'train' else data[split:]
        self.labels = labels[:split] if flag == 'train' else labels[split:]

    def __getitem__(self, i):
        return torch.tensor(self.data[i:i+96]), torch.tensor(self.labels[i+95]).unsqueeze(-1)
    def __len__(self): return len(self.data) - 100

# ==========================================
# 4. è®­ç»ƒå…¥å£
# ==========================================
def main():
    rank = int(os.environ["LOCAL_RANK"])
    torch.cuda.set_device(rank)
    dist.init_process_group("nccl")
    
    csv = 'real_btc_200mb.csv'
    train_ds = BTCDatasetExpert(csv, 'train')
    val_ds = BTCDatasetExpert(csv, 'val')
    num_vars = train_ds.data.shape[1] # è·å– 9 

    train_loader = DataLoader(train_ds, batch_size=256, sampler=DistributedSampler(train_ds))
    val_loader = DataLoader(val_ds, batch_size=256, sampler=DistributedSampler(val_ds, shuffle=False))

    model = Independent_Swin_iTransformer_V2(num_vars=num_vars).to(rank)
    model = DDP(model, device_ids=[rank])
    
    # ğŸ“‰ 5e-5 ä½å­¦ä¹ ç‡
    optimizer = torch.optim.AdamW(model.parameters(), lr=5e-5, weight_decay=1e-2)
    criterion = nn.BCEWithLogitsLoss()
    scaler = GradScaler('cuda')

    start_epoch = load_checkpoint(model, optimizer, scaler)

    if rank == 0: print(f"ğŸš€ Final Pro V2 å¯åŠ¨ | Vars: {num_vars}")

    for epoch in range(start_epoch, 20):
        train_loader.sampler.set_epoch(epoch)
        model.train()
        pbar = tqdm(train_loader, disable=(rank != 0), desc=f"Epoch {epoch+1}")
        for bx, by in pbar:
            bx, by = bx.to(rank), by.to(rank)
            optimizer.zero_grad()
            with autocast(device_type='cuda', dtype=torch.float16):
                loss = criterion(model(bx), by)
            scaler.scale(loss).backward()
            scaler.step(optimizer); scaler.update()

        model.eval()
        v_c, v_t = 0, 0
        with torch.no_grad():
            for bx, by in val_loader:
                bx, by = bx.to(rank), by.to(rank)
                with autocast(device_type='cuda', dtype=torch.float16): logits = model(bx)
                v_c += ((torch.sigmoid(logits) > 0.5).float() == by).sum().item()
                v_t += by.size(0)
        
        v_c_tensor, v_t_tensor = torch.tensor(v_c).to(rank), torch.tensor(v_t).to(rank)
        dist.all_reduce(v_c_tensor); dist.all_reduce(v_t_tensor)
        
        if rank == 0:
            print(f"ğŸ“Š Val Acc: {v_c_tensor.item()/v_t_tensor.item():.2%}")
            save_checkpoint(epoch, model, optimizer, scaler)

    dist.destroy_process_group()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
